			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '60a8dad2c4e6058574909dd289e5162a388f889d') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/classes/OIDplusDatabaseConnection.class.php');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('includes/classes/OIDplusDatabaseConnection.class.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/OIDplusDatabaseConnection.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusDatabaseConnection.class.php') != '1e93ba4b4c6b6f583f691da9c2f991c7df8bc33b') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusDatabaseConnection.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/OIDplusDatabaseConnection.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/OIDplusDatabaseConnection.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusDatabaseConnection.class.php') !== '1e93ba4b4c6b6f583f691da9c2f991c7df8bc33b') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusDatabaseConnection.class.php') !== '3262a2f2dfbf638fc68220df6e341bcf763cfe8c') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/classes/OIDplusDatabaseConnection.class.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/classes/OIDplusDatabaseConnection.class.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/classes/OIDplusDatabaseConnection.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplusDatabaseConnection.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusDatabaseConnection.class.php') !== '1e93ba4b4c6b6f583f691da9c2f991c7df8bc33b') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusDatabaseConnection.class.php');

	}

			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplusMenuUtils.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/functions.inc.php');
	writefile_7();
	if (!is_file('includes/functions.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/functions.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') != '337652d6516489fa310749a1e80e544b4eabf7ba') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/functions.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/functions.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/functions.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== '337652d6516489fa310749a1e80e544b4eabf7ba') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== '67ea3ce0ae3af9855e2588b538b0edb207493756') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/functions.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/functions.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/functions.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/functions.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_7();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== '337652d6516489fa310749a1e80e544b4eabf7ba') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/functions.inc.php');
		}
	}
}
